(Translated by Google) I had rented a Mustang for my brother for my birthday many months before. That day we brought my brother blindfolded there. Once there, everything was closed ..
Thank goodness someone came quickly and unlocked the shop. My brother was waiting outside and I went into the office to clear everything up. Once there, the landlord said that the Mustang is not there, it is in Vegas. Then he wanted to make me taste another car or talk me out of the Mustang. Then I got angry and explained the situation to him again that my brother, who was 30, was standing blindfolded outside and I had already paid for the Mustang. I then asked the boss because I no longer knew whether to cry or scream. This then came, apologized a thousand times. He then made the offer to drive the Audi r8 until the Mustang was there. I was absolutely not thrilled because we live where audi is made, but my brother became too impatient and I didn't want to argue any longer. So my brother got the r8 .. after an hour's drive my brother was called and finally he got his Mustang !!!!
He also had to pay because there were only 100 free miles !!
I could tell more but that's enough ..

He was very happy anyway, thank goodness .. but this company still doesn't get more than 2 stars from me !!

(Original)
Ich hatte für meinen Bruder zum Geburtstag einen Mustang gemietet schon viele Monate vorher. An dem besagten Tag haben wir meinen Bruder mit verbundenen Augen dort hingebracht. Dort angekommen war alles zu..
Gottseidank kam zügig jemand und sperrte den laden auf. Mein Bruder wartete draußen und ich ging rein ins Büro um alles zu klären. Drum angekommen sagte der Vermieter das der Mustang nicht da ist, der sei in Vegas. Dann wollte er mir ein anderes Auto schmackhaft machen bzw mir den Mustang ausreden. Dann wurde ich sauer und hab ihm die Situation nochmal erklärt das mein Bruder der seinen 30ten hat mit verbundenen Augen draußen steht und ich den Mustang doch schon bezahlt habe. Ich habe dann den Chef verlangt da ich nicht mehr wusste ob ich weinen oder schreien soll. Dieser kam dann, entschuldigte sich tausend mal. Dieser machte mir dann das Angebot erst den Audi r8 zu fahren bis der Mustang da ist. Ich war absolut nicht begeistert da wir dort wohnen wo audi hergestellt wird aber mein Bruder wurde zu ungeduldig und länger wollte ich auch nicht mehr streiten. Also erhielt mein Bruder den r8.. nach 1 Stunde fahrt wurde mein Bruder angerufen und endlich erhielt er seinen Mustang!!!!
Drauf zahlen musste er auch da es nur 100 freimeilen gab!!
Ich könnte noch mehr erzählen aber das reicht schon..

Er hat sich trotzdem sehr gefreut, gottseidank.. aber diese Firma bekommt trotzdem nicht mehr als 2 Sterne von mir!!<//review>

< Text>
Absolutely delicious and a must stop for anyone who enjoys fresh tasting, traditionally styled Mexican food. I had their Carnitas burrito that comes doused in a lovely tomatillo sauce and melted cheese, and it tasted even better than it looked, with rich buttery pork Carnitas that was so tender I barely had to chew.
I was entertained to find they serve their house made salsa in self serve syrup containers, and I found it very smart and fun to be able to so precisely control what I put on my plate. Their hotter salsa is also incredibly delicious, but it's a sneaky one that's builds heat, so use sparingly if you're not too big into spicy food.< /Text>

<rate>2</rate>< text>
I am really not sure how this place gets a four or five-star from anyone, but maybe I'm not the expert I think I am.

They had the old location at West and Myrtle that I reviewed long ago.
So I thought I would try the new location on Broadway just to see if anything had improved or gotten better.

I was sorely disappointed.

The old location at West and Myrtle that is now run under a new name and new ownership and New Management is much better than this restaurant.

Bad service; my accompanied guest found stuff in their water.

Took a long time just to get them to take our order. And there was a little bit of a language barrier not sure why?

I guess I came at a bad night because they were surprisingly busy and short-staffed.

The food was between a two and a three. Again my guest was even less impressed.

It's up to you. You take your own risk, I don't think it was worth the money.

I'm not going back for strike three.

To those who go there and absolutely love this place. I would say you need to visit the Bay Area and try some Hispanic restaurants down there or over in Redding to get a better idea what you're eating up here.

I don't know the ownership here I don't know the management. So this is not some kind of I got you kind of thing.

There are at least two other restaurants in Humboldt County that serve the same kind of food that is much much better, for a better price</text>

< review>
Horrible experience  -- 3 months delay to deliver a bed!

Would give 0 stars if possible

I ordered a bed frame in Dec 2019. The salesman in the store paired the wrong bed frame and headboard in the order, so when the bed arrived it couldn't be assembled. A technician who came to fix it thought the wrong screws had been delivered, so ordered them -- from the factory in Wisconsin.. 10 days to arrive, and when they did, of course did not solve the problem. When I complained a different tech ordered a new set of legs, --another 10 days to arrive, and again did not solve the problem.
At each visit to the store I was asked to wait at the customer service while a ticket was opened. Talked to the manager in person, and he couldn't help. The staff in the store seemed confused and kept passing the buck around about whose fault it was -- the factory in Wisconsin, the store etc.
After 2 months, the root cause was finally identified when they reviewed the original order. Then a new headboard was ordered --again 10 days to deliver. Finally got the bed set up in March 2020 --  3 months after the delivery!. No apology from the manager.

I observed the way the staff behaved during the whole episode -- the ladies at the front desk genuinely tried to help, but were hamstrung by their order process. The manager and other staff  could not identify the problem for a long time, and their discussions indicated they were just trying to point fingers.

Will never visit this location again.< /review>

They charged me for my living room and bedroom furniture, then started moving the delivery date back due to "back orders" or "not available in the warehouse." My living room was due to be delivered 5 days after purchase, 2 days prior to deliver they told me it would be 20 more days. 20 days with no living room furniture in my loft, no thank you.

The schedulers that call you will lie to you knowing you are not going to get your furniture when they promise it. I confirmed this with the folks in Folsom, I was made promises twice that were total BS. It's frustrating for the store employees too because it costs them sales.

It's a really crappy way to do business, but they already have your money so it's not a problem for them. Before setting up a delivery, confirm that you can pick up your purchases up in their warehouse the next day, if you can you will know they actually have it in stock and you can set up a delivery. I ended up making a deal where they sold me the floor samples off the floor and threw in an $800 love seat to make it right. Like I said, the folks in the store are awesome. As it is. my area rug that I paid for in July won't be available until September.<//Text><pictures>None<//pictures>< resp>

<Rate>1< /Rate><Review>We purchased an outdoor furniture set (glider, table, two chairs, rug, and throw pillows) that we saw in the Folsom store. The in-store guy we worked with was awesome. I told him originally we wanted to think it, and he gave us his cell. When I called him back on the last day of the sale, he was out, but he made sure we could still get the sale price, and we concluded the transaction on his return. When I forgot to call him on our arranged day, he reached out to us, which I appreciated.

That’s where the good part ends. When we got our delivery last Friday, the delivery team said our rug was on back order. This was news to us, and the delivery team was surprised we didn’t know this already. They had no estimate on when we'd get the rug. In addition, two of our cushions were missing, one of the throw pillows looked like it had some mud splattered on it, and one of our glider cushions looked like somebody with grease on their hands had handled every side. I don’t think it’s reasonable to expect that when you pay a lot for new stuff that the items should (1) arrive; and (2) be in new condition.

I called the delivery number at around 10 a.m. that Friday and explained my concerns, and the woman who I spoke with (while polite and empathetic) said she didn’t know how to handle my order. She asked if she could call me back. By 4:30 p.m. that day, I had heard nothing, so I called again. I was advised that when they got everything squared away, they would give me a call. It’s now 11 a.m. on Monday, and nobody has called. I have no idea what the status of my order is. But what I can say is that every time I've called, I was on hold for (no exaggeration) at least 20 minutes before I spoke to a human. In the aggregate, I have probably now spent 1.5 – 2.0 hours trying to remedy this issue. I am posting this YELP review in the hopes that someone with Ashley corporate will read it and resolve this issue without any communication except to email me when I am getting my stuff. I should not have to another second on it, in my opinion.< /Review>< pictures>
